## test NEGNAN : NEGNAN
ieee_test_1000 = {
    set_temp_variable = { comp_error_flag = 0 }

    set_temp_variable = { arg_a = -8388.607 }
    set_temp_variable = { arg_b = -8388.607 }

    set_temp_variable = { relation_output = 0 }
    if = {
        limit = {
            relationLess = yes
        }
        set_temp_variable = { relation_output = 1 }
    }

    set_temp_variable = { expected_output = 0 }

    set_temp_variable = { invalid = 0 }
    if = {
        limit = {
            check_variable = { comp_error_flag > 0 }
        }
        set_temp_variable = { invalid = 1 }
    }
    if = {
        limit = {
            OR = {
                NOT = { check_variable = { relation_output = expected_output } }
            }
        }
        set_temp_variable = { invalid = 1 }
    }
    if = {
        limit = {
            check_variable = { invalid = 1 }
        }
        log = "Test [?test_id] - NEGNAN !< NEGNAN - FAIL"
        add_to_temp_array = { test_fail_array = test_id }
    }
    else = {
        log = "Test [?test_id] - NEGNAN !< NEGNAN - PASS"
    }

    log = "Actual: [?relation_output]"
    log = "Expect: [?expected_output]"
    
    set_temp_variable = { comp_error_flag = 0 }
}
